et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	 And do not press with your hand, but rather hold it openly as if smelling something.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	 And some old people say that some men use a cautery like a razor, and heat it and insert it between the ribs until it reaches that abscess.
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	 And so it is with pain, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	 But in this work there is danger that the patient may die now or a fistula may occur which cannot be healed.
de la mice	 of the urine
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	 When you treat the disease of urine according to what we have said in the sections on treatments, and it does not benefit, then there are three ways of fire cautery which are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	 From which there is a manner such that you make three or four cauteries, lining according to the length of the bladder, according to the shape of the liver cautery that we have said before;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	 And do not press your hand onto the entire cautery, and let the patient be leaning on their back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	 And another manner of cautery is that you heat the cautery which has two nerves, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	 And lift the scrotum which is near the bladder, or the side of the patient comes towards the left, and let the elevation by which you lift the scrotum be according to the size, according to the length of the body, and the cauteries be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	 Afterwards, he applies two inflamed nerves so that the heart is pierced from the other side, and then draws out through the cautery, and thus there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	 And if you see, then cauterize the entire cautery with three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	 After the treatment when it has excreted pus for a long time, and this is different from the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	 of the dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	 Cautery is not beneficial to those with dropsy, except in the manner called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	 When you heal according to the manners that we have said in divisions, and your healing does not profit at all, then it is necessary that you make four cauteries around the buttocks, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the bladder, two behind the back on the spine, and one in the place of the breast;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	 and let the cautery be very close to the heart's breadth.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	 Afterwards, leave the cautery open for a long time to release pus, and do not neglect the patient's care after the cautery;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	 And if healing is hastened, then the two intentions will be together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	 The form of the cautery for the stomach should be the tool that we have previously shown;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	 And that for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what is placed here before.
de l’enfleure des piez	 Of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	 When the feet are swollen in one who is dropsical and full of citrin urine, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the little finger and the ring finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	 And lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	 Et ne pénètre pas trop profondément, ainsi tu risquerais de toucher l'os citrin, et que le fer à cautériser soit conforme à cette forme:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	 After that, make two cauteries on each leg at the tip of the shinbone;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	 And let one of the long cauteries be below the knee in front and the other behind, in the middle of the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	 And let the cauteries heal over slowly without cure, for the awl comes out.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	 after the cure of other wounds that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	 de la ménopause
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	 When an intestinal solution comes from cold and moisture, to the point that the retentive and digestive virtues in the stomach and intestines are weakened, and cannot be cured by ordinary means of treatment;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	 and you see the patient well-tolerating and of strong virtue, then make a great cautery on the stomach according to what has been said before in the stomach cautery, in the circular cautery.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	 and four subtle cauteries around the navel, each one subtly clavicle, and two cauteries on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	 And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, make a cautery on the wrist, and one cautery on each eye, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large one, for the cure is beneficial when there is good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	 of the cure for hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	 When hemorrhoids are in the anus, one or several, and they are old and consist of large, cold, moist, corrupted humors, and they are treated as we have said in sections, and it does not help, then make cauteries.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	 Three on the spine of the back, which are entirely below the navel, point by point in a triangle, and one cautery below the anus two fingers.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	 And if you think that his stomach is cooled and the meat does not cook, and one sees the face swell, then on the face place one great cautery on the stomach, as was said before, and another on the liver, and another on the bladder with all the cauteries closed.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	 And let the cautery remain open for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After the cure of the place until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	 of the fleshiness which is named "tegula
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	 When you cut the nail, heat the cautery that looks like a razor, and then place it entirely ablaze on that cut nail;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	 and leave your hand there until the cautery comes to the base of the vein, so that the blood flow is stopped;
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	 do this once or twice, and if there is much nail, cauterize each one as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	 afterwards, care for the wounds until they are healed;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	 and if you cauterize with a large cautery on top of gold, it will have greater benefit.
de plaie mal curee	 of a poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	 When the patient cannot tolerate cutting or opening, which we will explain in its place, such illness occurs that cannot be healed except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	 When someone gets a fistula, and it is open and emits foul and corrupt moisture, you should probe it all with a fine tent, and make sure that you know the depth of the entire tent.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	 Afterwards, heat the cautery that looks like a razor and insert it into the fistula according to the amount that the tent has entered, and restart the cautery until that rotten and corrupted flesh is burnt, once, or twice, or three times, according to how much is needed;
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	 And guard yourself against drawing out the nerves that are within, and from large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	 If the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and the intestines, guard yourself against these places, and do not perform such fevers except in a fleshy place, and consider that it is not persistent;
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	 After curing the place until it is healed, and if the place is healthy and the matter has been removed for a long time, then know that the place is completely healed;
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	 And if the matter is not removed, know that the place is torn, and the bone is corrupt at its root.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	 And thus as one of those which we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	 of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	 When pain from cold comes to the kidneys, and from a great flatulence, and she does not want intercourse, then it is necessary that you make a cautery on the kidneys on one side and the other with the clavicle cautery that we have previously mentioned;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	 And if we cauterize in the middle, she will have three cauteries in a line, and they will be of greater help.
de la vessie	 of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	 When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then make a cautery on the opposite side above the bladder, where the pubic hair begins, one to the right and one to the left, and let each cautery be as long as the thumb of a man.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	 And make the cautery on the back, or two if you need it.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	 And let the cautery be clavicle according to the shape previously mentioned.
de la marris	 Of the uterus
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	 When the womb is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	 And when they come, there is great pain.
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	 Then it is necessary to make three cauteries around the navel, as we have said in the bladder cautery, and two on the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	 And let the cautery be clavicle, as we have said.
de la hainche	 Of the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	 When the viscous moisture descends to the hipbone, and for this reason it moves from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	 And the place of separation is found, then you must cauterize the patient on the hip bone with a circular cautery, and sign before the place around the bone as it turns, so that the bone is within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	 And let the cautery be such as that with which one has cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	 And if this cautery is not present, make three large olive cauteries, and let the cautery be as deep as all the hearts.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And care for it until it heals.
de la dolor de la hainche	 Of hip pain
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	 When pain comes in the hip bone and it is due to cold and moisture, and the patient is treated with what we have said in the division and the treatment does not help, and the disease is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	 then it is necessary that you purge the patient of heavy humors with stinking pills, or other good similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	 Afterwards, make a cautery on him;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	 and the manner of the cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	 that is to say, with burning medicines together, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	 Fire cautery is according to many methods, one of which is as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	 you should cauterize on the hipbone three triangular cauteries in this manner, and make them deep and large, and let there be between each cautery a space as thick as a finger, and let the cautery be olive-sized;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	 sometimes one makes a cautery in the middle on top of the hipbone, for which there are four, like this:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	 And if you see, then cauterize it with the circular cautery that we have previously mentioned for hip dislocation;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	 but do it in such a way that the circle contains the entire hip, and all the thickness of the flesh is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	 And this is the manner in which one proceeds in sciatica, when the pain is located in the hip, and does not extend to the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	 And if it goes as far as the thigh and the leg, then make two cauteries there where the patient says he feels pain, and one cautery above the ankle at four fingers' width, a little to the left side;
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	 and let the cautery be cupped, and let the thickness of the flesh be burned.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	 and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two fingers of the foot or near there, then cauterize where he feels the pain with three or four points at the cautery which is called "point".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	 And if necessary, do more of them;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	 And if he knows that the pain is beneath the knee towards the thigh, make him a knife or circular cautery, and take good care in all your cauteries not to leave the cautery so long that you burn the nerves and large arteries, and thus cause more harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	 And I myself have seen many who have made a cautery on the ankle of the foot, and left it for so long that the entire leg was swollen, as well as the foot, which was then punctured and rotted completely.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	 After a colic from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	 And if the pain is in two places together, make a cautery in one and in the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	 And the wise say that for the hip cautery, which is of this kind, make such an iron and let it be at the tip as thick as a penny or a little less, and let it be barbed, and from one barb to the other let there be the thickness of a pea.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	 And let the assistants be in two parts, and also like knots, and there should be one handle of iron well-made.
et c’est li forme:	 And this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	 And let it be heated until it is all red and glowing, and then place it on the sore of the ill hip, and turn it over onto the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	 And the cautery once, the cautery returns and leave it for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	 And then make a poultice of butter, and leave the wound open for a long time.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 After the care of dressing until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	 Al-Zahrawi says that we use little of this cautery because of the fear of its appearance, and if one sees little who uses it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	 And yet this is of good cauterizations, which he can endure, and there where it fits.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	 The cautery of medicine is such that you make the instrument between the teeth in which descends the margin of the door, and let it be of brass or iron with one long side, and at the height have II holes, and between each the size of a finger's thickness;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	 And they should be open from without and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	 Afterwards, place the box of the hip on the patient lying on his healthy side, and then your hand very high on the box of the hip;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	 afterwards throw between the two circles of the hot water which should be heated over the fire with a bag, and let it stay for an hour, and let the patient endure the heat and burning of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	 Because there is biting, as if by fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	 and when the biting has passed, lift your hand with the instrument and gently raise the hip; leave it thus for three days, and apply butter until what is blackened by the burn is removed;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	 and let it sit for three days so that pus can be drawn out.
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and this would be the last aid after the treatment of onion until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	 And if the pain has spread to the thigh or the leg, make an instrument that dyes with alum in the same way that you have done on the hip.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	 And this is the manner of hot alum, and I have written it in the treatise on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	 Take quicklime and live coal, as much of one as the other, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	 And if there is a small hole except for where the point of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	 and put another well-sealed pot on top of it, and put alkali, heat, and sweet water on top, so that there are two powders on top until you have well held it in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	 and leave it thus until the water descends into the sealed pot, then take all that water and throw it on heat and on alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	 And then it will be very hot and is used in many works of medicine and in the cautery of other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	 For it performs the same work as fire, and there are other medications with which one can cauterize the hip well thus, such as terebinth resin, honey of cardamom, heat with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	 And Galen tells us of a treatment whereby a man was healed from the pain in his hip and sciatic vein, praising it greatly, saying that no other treatment was done, and that he was cured at once when this treatment was performed, and then he bathed as is taught hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	 And says in such a way that you take green and dry tin, and grind it very well with a little fat, and place it on the hip and thigh and leg where the pain is, and leave it there.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	 And let it remain for three hours, until the patient no longer feels the burning sensation.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	 And then have him enter the bath so that his body is slightly warmed, and put him to bed, and all the pain will leave, and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	 Et sachez que nul ne doit user de cautère de telles médecines, si ce n'est après l'évacuation du corps.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	 And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat hairs, it helps greatly.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	 and the cautery should be done in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	 Prenez de la laine et badigeonnez-la d'huile vieille, puis placez-la sur la fosse située entre le gros orteil et le suivant, appelée fossile.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	 Afterwards, take dry goat hairs and hold them in the fire until they are charred, and place them on wool, and leave them until they are stained;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	 and do it again in this way, and do not stop doing so until you feel that it reaches the hip, and that the pain ceases;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	 And this manner of cautery is called "cautery of goat.
de la dolor dou dos	 Of back pain
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	 When pain comes to the back, from falling or blows or too great evacuation, or similar to cold matter spread, for none of these reasons is it worth using cautery, except for that which comes from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	 It is necessary that after the patient has been purged with stinking pills or other similar things, one makes on his back, where the pain is, three lines signified by an inch, and in each line V cauteries or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can bear;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	 And let the cautery be done according to the cautery which is called "point";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	 and if you see fit, do III or IV cauteries at the midpoint of the nail-shaped cautery according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	 Often this disease occurs in small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have a narrow forehead when they wake up, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	 And you will find at the end of the spine on the back, and we see an appearance that comes over the other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	 When you see this, and wish to cure it, then cauterize with the hot iron according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	 So that the iron touches each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	 And if you wish, then cauterize around the spine with a pointed iron two or three lines, and let the points be close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	 After curing the place until it is healed as we have said, beware that you do not apply cautery in a place where there is a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	 of joint pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	 When the pain of the joints is due to moisture that spreads throughout each member of the body, and when pain comes in the feet, which physicians call "gout" properly, and when it is caused by cold and cannot be cured with medicines, it is cured by cautery in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	 Make many cauteries around the joint of the foot, and let the cautery be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	 And if it is necessary that you cauterize on the surface of the foot, then make a full cautery at what is called the "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	 And if the pain extends to the knees and other joints, which often happens, then make three or four cauteries on each knee from each side, making the entire cautery olive-shaped.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	 And if you need more, do it more, but do not hold your hand outside the length of the heart's blade.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	 And if the pains descend as far as the knee and the back, then administer the cautery that we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	 And if the pain is in the hands, make an incision around the wrist two lines long;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	 and if there remains any pain in the fingers, make an incision on each joint and on the palm of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	 And if the pain reaches the ribs or the shoulders, cauterize each part, and take good care of the patient and administer medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	 For if you take good care of him and purge phlegm, he will be healed with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	 of the rupture of the shoulder
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	 When vomiting comes in waves, and the bowels descend into the kidneys and this is recent, it should be that when you see him being treated, he should not eat that day;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	 And that he uses things which cause wind to leave, so that the feces descend from his stomach;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	 after that make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to take his thighs until the buttocks are repaired, and bring them together with your fingers, and sign from below the root above the wrist bone, and all in one sign which should be similar to half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 then heat the cautery with what is used for this purpose:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	 until it becomes white and falls out.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	 Then reset the buttocks in their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	 and the practitioner should take his hand such that they do not return behind.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	 and firmly hold the thighs of the patient, and place a pillow and a bolster under the thighs, and another one under the feet which he should hold with his hands; ︎
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	 Then place the cautery on the sign as much of your hand as possible, and hold it straight and firm until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat it again until you reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	 And be careful that the boil does not burst when you apply the cautery.
que tu ne le brulasses;	 so that you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	 and so that the patient does not die from this or suffer other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	 And know that when you do not go as far as the bone with the cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	 And it is necessary that the cautery for children be fine according to their size, and also large for adults according to their size.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	 after three days, cure the place of the cautery with butter until the burn is gone.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	 after curing with other ointments until it is healed, let the patient lie on their back for forty days until the wound is well healed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	 And it is necessary that his nursing be prolonged for a long time, so that the boils do not burst when he tries to go into rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	 And after forty days, when he wishes to get up, let him be provided with a well-made splint, and carry it for another forty days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	 and let him have good rest, that he work little and guard against too great repletion of drinking and eating, and from laughing too loudly.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	 And when he does this teaching, then he is completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	 And I will say hereafter the treatment of cutting in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	 of belly rupture
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	 When ruptures come in other bellies and are known, and you see that they do not grow anymore, let him make the cautery of the cautery again according to its size, and let it be burned a third of the heart.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	 after the treatment as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	 and some of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized with a three-pronged cautery according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	 but first mark the place of the cut and make a line across the width above the rupture, and another below, and then place your hand in the middle with the whole cautery nailed.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	 But the first cautery is lighter and easier.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	 Of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	 When pain comes to any limb, from falling or striking, and this pain lasts for a long time, and the cure of medicine is not effective, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called "poin
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	 if it is healed from the first cautery, that is good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	 if this is not the case, commence another cautery on top of it, for such is the custom that it should move to the nearest member, therefore you must do the cauteries until the patient is healed.
de meselerie	 of mixture
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	 Mixtures are sometimes helped by cautery with great benefit, and likewise the diseases that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and black bile.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	 When you see her being cauterized, take care if the illness is at the beginning, and if it is cured according to what we have said in the division, and does not abate or stop, and you doubt that corruption will spread throughout the patient, then make five cauteries on the head: ‌
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	 I insert the needle into the head at the nape, and the other towards the forehead at the hairline.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	 and the second above the two temples, and one behind on the occiput.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	 and let your hand be such that the cautery reaches the bone, and so that the scabs come out freely so that the vapors of the gross humors can exit.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	 and cauterize on the bladder according to what was before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	 And if the disease is scattered everywhere;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	 and it clearly worsens, then you must cauterize with these cauteries that we have mentioned on the head, and one cautery at the base of the nose, and two cauteries on the spine of the neck, and six cauteries on the spine of the back, and one large one on the buttocks and another nearby, and two on each shoulder.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	 And two on each rib, and two on each tendon of the foot, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands.
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	 And be careful not to burn the nerves that are on the lower part of the spine.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	 And sometimes one performs a cautery on the bone of the wrist, and one on the bone of the stomach, and one on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	 And know that the more cauteries are performed, the more help is provided, and the greater the benefit.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	 And know that the patient does not feel pain from the cautery as the healthy person feels it, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	 And it is necessary that the cauteries be large and small according to the members and the joints, as you will find in the manner of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	 After the cure, treat the place with flour of peas mixed with honey and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	 When swelling comes to any member and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then make cauteries on the member according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	 and let the cautery be a little inside the thickness of the heart.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then the treatment should continue until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	 And sometimes one performs the cautery both on the hand and on the foot and on the back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus the swelling is removed.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	 yet no one should interfere with it unless they are knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the nerves that move the body.
de albaras	 Of cauterizing
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	 When the disease called "albaras" is aggravated and medicinal remedies have no effect, then one should cauterize with a cautery that is a little deep, according to the thickness of the heart, until the whiteness is removed and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	 Then take flour of vetch and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and blood of a pigeon and blood of an almond tree, one part each;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And let it all be mixed together, and bound with a cloth, and applied to the place until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	 The treatment of cancer by means of cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	 When cancer first appears and you see it stop, then cauterize it with a circular cautery all around the tumor.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	 Yet the wise say that one should also make a cautery in the middle of the cancer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	 yet this does not seem good to me, for I fear that it may become ulcerated and corrupt, and I have seen it happen sometimes.
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	 And a more proper thing is that it be cauterized around it, with the cautery that is called "circular," as we have said in many cauteries.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	 of the swelling that cannot subside
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	 When someone has a disease called "adubelati," it delays death either due to the excess of the disease or because of the weakness of the patient when he is old and lacks blood, or due to time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	 and you see that it hastens death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	 then cauterize around it with many small cauteries by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	 afterwards, leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	 Because she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	 And if you see her pierce through the entire cautery, then heat the cautery as follows:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	 And place your hand in the middle of this illness called "adubelati" so that the cautery pierces through to the heart, and let the cautery be such that the patient feels it on the surface in such a way that the course of the corruption is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 After the treatment until he is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	 The fire cure by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	 There is another type of illness called "corrodens," and it is nothing other than the consumption of a limb, for it consumes the limbs just as fire does dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	 If you see this disease in a place that can bear the fire of cautery together, then heat up the cauteries, both small and large, according to what is needed for the place where the disease is;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	 afterwards, cauterize from all sides until you remove all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, so that everything that is corrupt may be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	 And then leave it for III days, and apply a soft bandage with oil on the cauterized places until the burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	 After the treatment of burning wounds producing flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	 And if after three days healthy flesh does not grow, this is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	 and if not, then restart the cautery on that which remains of the corrupt place.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	 And this disease has sometimes been cured by liquid medicine instead of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	 but nevertheless, fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already described the treatment with liquid medicine in the section (on that topic).
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	 take as much as you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	 of leeks that grow near the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	 It often happens that on the soles of the feet, according to our understanding, there grows a disease called "tumor," which is a large, hairy growth that hurts the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	 And the cautery for this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	 That is to say, fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	 Fire cautery is that you heat the cautery like it is a feather of an owl, and it should be made of good iron to the measure that it can pierce the nail from all sides, and there should be subtle edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	 after placing everything hot on the nail, turn your hand completely around the nail until it reaches the head of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	 and leave it there for three days until it begins to putrefy.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	 then make a poultice of crushed wild mallows with silk and leave the poultice on all night, and the nail will fall out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat the site of burn with warm ointment until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	 And if they are turned outward on the body, and this often happens in hands and feet, you should apply a hot water cautery to it.
et est en teil maniere:	 and it is done in this manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	 take a reed of iron or brass, or a goose quill, and place it on the nail and the wart, that is to say, on the small warts.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	 and put the chain on so that it touches all around, then place a pouch of hot water on it, hold your hand well, and press your hand in circles so that the edge of the chain reaches the base of the nail, and let the hot water find its deep way to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	 and let the patient bear the scalding of the hot water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	 then leave it like that, and it will be uprooted from all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	 Thus do one after another, so that you exhaust all those which are in the body, then cure the wounds which produce flesh.
li cure dou trembler	 cure the trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	 When someone trembles from cold of the nerves, or from quartan fever or another, then you must make four or three cauteries on the spine of the back, one cautery between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	 And in the case of cautery on the foot, and also on the stomach for the liver cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	 it will cause the body to shake, and speed up the healing process from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	 stinking pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	 Sometimes appear on the outside of the body as baths or stinking pustules, which come from large corrupt substances.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	 if necessary at first when they appear, then cautery should be performed on each head of the boil:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	 a subtle cautery made from myrtle wood, with the tip grasped in fire, or a long root of Aristolochia, or a lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	 And sometimes they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear in this manner, and they cannot grow afterwards, but the superfluousness from which they come is dissolved, and the person is healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	 But this must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	 when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	 Often there is a great loss of blood from the artery that is cut in the wound that comes to the surface, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the cautery of the limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	 And it is a very serious matter to lose blood.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	 And yet when this happens to someone, you must hurry to put your finger on the vein of the wound, and press it very hard until the blood stops flowing under your finger, so that no drop comes out anymore;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	 then put on the fire several small and large olive-shaped cauteries until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	 Then take I, whether large or small according to the wound and the place where the vessel is cut, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, and hold the cautery until the blood is coagulated.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	 And if it spurts when you lift your finger from the vein and the cautery is extinguished, then quickly take another one of the cauteries that are in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	 And do not stop doing this one after another until the blood is stopped;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	 and beware that you do not burn the nerve that is nearby, and that no other evil comes upon the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	 and know that when the blood flows from the artery, it cannot be well coagulated, even if the artery is large, except by one of the four methods that we have said:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	 or by cautery, or by extraction if it is not treated, or by tightly binding with thread, or by applying medicines that have the power to coagulate blood.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	 And it must be bound and held firmly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	 Whoever administers stopping by tightly tying cloth or putting hot things on it, or other similar things, if it does not benefit, it can be of no use.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	 And if this happens to anyone and he does not have a mirror or medicine at hand, then he must put his finger tightly on the vein's wound as we have said, and press firmly until it is constricted above the wound and above the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	 And do not move the finger, but frequently apply cold water until it is very cold and the blood becomes thickened and constricted.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	 And make inquiries beforehand about those who need cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	 Here begins the second book of the cure for wounds
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	 We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases that require fire cautery or hot medicines, and the questions and causes, and the instruments and forms of cauterization.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	 And I have placed this chapter from the top of the head to the feet, and I will proceed in this chapter by the same route so that one may find more easily what one seeks.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	 And before I begin this, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauterizations, and for this reason greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	 For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	 where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	 And I warn you not to undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	 For many kinds of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	 if they are of such a nature that they have taken care of themselves with their illness to the point where they die quickly because of the madness that they experience from their illness and the severity of their sickness.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	 And of these one should have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	 And there are some who give you their mind, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	 "wait, I am healed";
et li maladie est despitouse.	 and the illness is spiteful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	 You should not agree with those who come to you in this manner, but put more importance on your honor than on your greed. Do not open yourself foolishly, but wisely to that of which you are certain and from which you can receive benefit and praise.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	 and use prognosis and diagnosis in the treatment of your patients, so that health may be restored;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	 and this will help you to acquire good renown, glory, and praiseworthy memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	 Very dear son, may our Lord grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you wish to aspire from the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	 Now I have arranged this chapter in discussions by chapters, following what is before the chapter on cauteries, which I have discussed from the head to the feet, so that you may find more easily that of which you will have need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	 full of water from the head
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	 You should know that this disease often comes to children during childbirth, and when the midwife holds the baby's head too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	 and sometimes it happens for no apparent reason.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	 And I have never seen this disease except in children, and in all the cases I have seen, death comes quickly.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	 Therefore, it seems to me that I should refrain from treating such cases.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	 And I saw a child whose head was full of water, and the head swelled each day so that he could not support it.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	 and the moisture increased so much that he died, and this moisture is collected under the bone on the forehead, between the brain and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	 And the operation is such that if there is moisture between the heart and the bone, and the abscess is small, you should cut a wide slit in the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	 and let it be as long as two fingers, until the moisture flows out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	 and see here the shape of the spatula:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	 If the moisture is more abundant, and the abscess is larger, then make two cuts in the shape of a cross, as shown in this figure.
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	 And if the moisture is under the bone, and you see the seams of the head open on each side, and the water jumps out strongly when you press it with your hand inside, and this is not answered to you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	 then you must cut three slits in the head like this:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	 And after the incision, draw out all the moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	 After closing the slits with lint and powder, put wine and oil on them, and leave it like this until the fifth day.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	 Then dislocate it, and treat the wound with compresses and ointments, and let the head be pulled evenly, and then give the patient dry food of little moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	 And another method of incision is that you observe where the abscess opens and the gathering of pus;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	 for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	 sometimes behind;
aucune fois en destre;	 sometimes to the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	 and sometimes to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	 Therefore cut there where the abscess opens, and the accumulation of pus, and make the incision according to what you can do about it;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	 and beware that you do not cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	 And let there be a flow of blood, so that the patient may die from loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	 De la règle
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	 Lorsqu'il arrive à quelqu'un une maladie appelée «catarrhe» aux yeux ou au sein, et que la maladie est ancienne, et que le traitement par médicaments ne profite pas, alors le dernier recours est la cautérisation avec ce dont on coupera les deux artères.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	 Therefore, when you see them covered, the patient should lean back.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	 After rubbing the area with a rough cloth until the veins appear, the patient should pull their neck taut against the entire cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	 then look where the vein beats, and the location of one and the other are behind the ears, and they are found rarely;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	 then mark the places with ink, then cover each one with a sharp spatula of two parts, as deep as the cut goes to the bone, and this should be done across the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	 And if you see, push the spatula underneath the artery and cut above it, cutting as one should across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	 And when the vein is cut, the blood jumps up continuously outward.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	 And if the artery does not open to touch, then you must measure the quantity of the space of three fingers' width, then take hold and cut down to the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	 And that which should be put out of the blood is six ounces, and perhaps a little more or less, according to what the patient can endure, and the filling of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	 Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 If there remains a point on the bone like a spike, then cut it so that such abscesses do not come there; then press the wound and bind it, and continue the care of bandaging until it is healed.
de emigrainne	 of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	 Quant old age comes, and acute catarrh, due to the moisture of tears and heat in the temples, and ancient insanity and similar things, and it is treated by various methods of medicine and all this does not benefit him at all, then we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have said.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	 And the manner of their extraction is that the patient should let the hair on his temples grow long, and pay attention to the artery that opens in the temple, for it opens well with its pulsing, and it protrudes little outside except in some men who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	 and if it is broken, let the patient pull its neck with some cloths, then rub the place with some rough cloth, and rinse the place with hot water until the artery appears clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	 then take the spoon of which there is the form here:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	 then lightly scrape the skin until you reach the artery, then draw it up with forceps, and carefully separate it from the tissues that are underneath each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	 and if the artery is thin, turn it with the point of the hook, then cut that part according to the quantity of the two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	 For if it is not cut, then the blood does not stop at all.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	 And draw blood for the VI c/j until III;
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	 and if the artery is large, it is necessary that you tie it in two places with a strong double silk thread, so that putrefaction does not occur before the wound is healed, and let the blood flow out gradually.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	 Then cut the excess that is between the two ligaments in that same hour, and then, if you see fit, use the cautery knife to cauterize down to the bone until the joints are severed.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	 And this is a moderate work, if the patient does not have fever and has a warm temperament.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	 Because the cautery serves to dry out moisture:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	 for this reason it is of great help against moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	 Where, for the extraction of arteries, one should fill the place with old cotton and apply well-made bandages on top.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when they are unwrapped, let them be treated with dry medications that promote the growth of flesh and bandages until they heal.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And if there is no bleeding from the artery as long as you work there, then hasten to use the copper with the caustic, and apply it to the place where you have put the vitriol and hold it in your hand until the blood is cauterized.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	 And if you do not have this available, then place your finger on the spot until the blood is frozen, and wash the spot with cold water until the bleeding stops, and hold it as needed.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	 And one who is more skilled and lighter in extracting the artery is that you should cauterize the wound with this sharp caustic from two sides, but let the incisions be well spaced to retain their heat longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	 Because when the instrument is too damp, it retains less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	 And there should be a finger's width between the two knives, and then when you have burned both places with the hot iron until it reaches the bone, and cut the wound in two places.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	 And let there be a space between the two heads, for it is not fused by this cautery entirely.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	 and this is the form of the cautery:
des larmes	 tears
