et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	 And if it is not healed, or the incision is not entirely made, because the patient does not want to rest, or due to blood flow, then you must fill the wound with damp cotton and a corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	 And leave it until it melts away the rest and the fat, then treat it until it is healed.
des apostemes des asselles	 of the abscesses of the armpits
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	 This abscess that comes under the armpits is like hard scrofula with bones, and there are some that contain moisture.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	 Those that contain moisture should be cut in this shape, from line b to line g:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when all the pus that is in the abscess has been emptied, fill the wound with old cotton, and leave it until the next day, then remove all the cotton, and treat with suitable ointment until it heals.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	 And if the abscess is similar to scrofula, incise it as we have said for scrofula incisions, and if the wound exudes pus, apply cautery as we have said before.
de la routure de l’artere	 of the rupture of the artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	 When the artery has burst and the skin on top is closed, it often happens that abscesses form, and it also happens in the case of a swollen vein and an abscess;
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	 And if one knows this way when it is by the artery, then the abscess is long and deep.
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	 And when you feel it with your two fingers, you sense the constriction.
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	 And when it is by the vein, then the abscess appears very red.
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	 And it is foolish to cut this abscess, especially when it is under the armpits and in the joints and in the neck and in many other places, and it is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	 Therefore, it is necessary to avoid the use of fire cautery, and one who is chief should also avoid it, and in the case of inflammation of the artery, make an incision above the skin along its length.
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	 Then proceed with the cutting as usual, and neatly separate the artery from the tissues until it is exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	 Then push under him an awl, and make it pierce through to the other side, and tie off the artery with a double thread in two places, just as I have taught you in the extraction of the two arteries that are in the temples.
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	 Then prick the place between the two ligatures with a probe until the pus comes out, and let the abscess be relieved.
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	 Then proceed with the care that should follow afterward, until the ligature falls off.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then treat it as for an infection, until it is healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	 And if the abscess is because of the size of the vein, it is necessary that you take into your hand whatever you can from the abscess on all the skin. Then push the awl under the place that you hold in your hand, and make it pierce through to the other side; and there should be a double thread so that you draw it out from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	 Then tie the abscess, as I have told you, with a thread between two of its extremities.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	 and if you doubt that the thread will not hold firmly, then insert another needle through all of the thread underneath the entire abscess at the incision of the first needle, and tighten the thread in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	 then cut away the abscess until the pus comes out, then cut away the pus from the core and leave that which is tied.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then place a cloth soaked in wine and oil on it, then provide dressings of lint and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	 of nerve abscesses
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	 Similarly, as an abscess can occur in the artery and vein, so too can an abscess form in the nerves when they are wounded or subjected to excessive strain, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	 And this happens most often in the shoulders and arms, and in all places where there are joints, and these are serious abscesses, and their color resembles that of flesh, and they are in many forms without pain.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	 And when one strongly stretches it, then the patient feels pain, which is not in the depth of the body, but beneath the heart.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	 and it moves well on all sides, neither forward nor backward, nor below nor above, and that which is in the joints must not be struck with iron.
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	 perhaps there will be contraction.
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	 And that which is on the head or forehead, make the skin into a small pouch.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	 If the abscess is small, then hold it with tongs and strike at its root.
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if it is large, then suspend it to the hook, and scrape it off, then remove it and sew up the wound with stitches, and treat it until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	 of hanging boils
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	 Sometimes it occurs in the belly and not elsewhere, and it is an illness called "fungus" because of its similarity to mushrooms, and it has a subtle root and a large head.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	 And there are some small ones and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	 And I have seen a man who had two in his belly that were more like mushrooms than anything else, and there was no difference between them, and they were white, and had thin roots, and were always moist.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	 I cut them and found that one weighed eighteen ounces and the other six pounds, and the operation in the incision is such that you should consider if the patient is moist, and the color of the tumor is white and moist with a subtle root.
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	 If he strikes the spatula broadly, and let the cautery be in your presence with fire.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	 For in cutting often comes a too great outpouring of blood, and if the blood overcomes you, then hasten with cauterization.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	 And if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the iron incision, then take a well-made thread of linen and bind it around the wound as we have said, and leave it for two days.
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	 And then bind it tightly, and do not stop pulling the linen thread until he cuts the wound, and each time without difficulty.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	 And if the roots are large, there is fear of cutting into the intestines, but you can cut half, then cauterize it so that it does not return.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	 Then treat the wound, and take care not to cut the thin layer that is of a dark color, weak sensation, and milky appearance.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	 Car this is an encrusted boil, and I will come to the cure of boils later.
quant li boude ist fuer	 When the pustule is strong
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	 If the swelling of the abdomen comes from cauterizing a wound or a skin cut, and it is on the stomach and in some other areas as happens in other injuries, or from blood that flows from veins or arteries as described above, or from flatulence;
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	 and if it is from the injury of the skin and the excretion of pus, then the color of the abscess resembles the color of the body, and it is a light thing without pain, and it opens in various places.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	 And if it is from the issue of the intestine, then it is more varied, and when one presses it with their fingers, it resists, and then returns, and perhaps swells, and greatly increases at the entrance to the bath and due to intense labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	 And if it is from moisture, it is a light thing, and when you press it with your hand, it gives way well, without any resistance;
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	 And if it is due to blood, the abscess reveals these signs: it is large and hard, and fixed according to a certain measure.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	 And if it is due to flatulence, it is soft to the touch, and the operation is such that you must consider whether the appearance is of blood from an artery or a vein, or of flatulence.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	 Then you must leave the treatment.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	 For there is doubt and fear, as I have told you in the chapter on abscesses, concerning the artery and the vein.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	 And if the appearance is of the intestines or stomach, you must instruct the patient to take a bath and lie straight, then sign all around the abdomen.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	 then command them to lie down between your hands, and go around the marked area with all the spatial awareness, then extend half of the abscess upward with all the large hooks.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	 Then tie the limb around with a strong thread or a sturdy silk rope firmly, and let the knot be tight.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	 Then work the half of the abscess stretched over the ligature, and insert your finger into it, and seek the intestines.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	 If you find it trapped by the ligature, then loosen it, and insert the intestine out of the belly;
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	 And if you find the bowel, then take it by the end, and cut off the excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	 And if the artery or vein opposes you, then go around it well, then return to your work and take two needles, and put two strong threads in them, and put the two needles around what you have done in a cross as you made it pierce.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	 Then restrain the abscess in four places with needles, and if you see, remove the needles, and let the place until it suppurates, and each of the dead flesh will fall off by itself.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	 or cut it when it has been softened and suppurated, then treat as needed, and remove the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	 and drain the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the place as needed, and stitch up the place.
dou chancre	 Of the cancer
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	 We have said in the division the similarities of cancer, and how one should work with it using medicines, and how one must avoid treatment with iron.
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	 and we say that cancer begins in the flesh, and great caution is needed in its treatment, and the ancients said that when a cancer is in a place where it can be scraped off, such as a cancer on the breast, or on the thigh, or in similar places, it should all be removed when it is in the beginning.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	 And when it is large and old, then you must not approach it, for I have never seen anyone heal from it.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	 Nor has anyone ever healed from it before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	 And the work, when it is in place where one can remove it, as we have said, is that you should purge the patient of black bile some time.
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	 then make him fast if he has evident fullness, then put the patient in a good place to perform the work.
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	 then throw away your nails and scabies, and shave all parts, and remove it from all parts without leaving anything behind.
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 and let the blood flow freely, and press well the place with your hand or any other thing, and if the continuous bleeding hinders the incision of the artery or vein, then cauterize it until the blood is stopped.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then treat him with another treatment until he is healed.
de ydropisie	 of the dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	 We have already spoken in the division about the resemblances of dropsy, and in what manner the gathering of water is done, and the signs of each resemblance, and the treatment that is done by medicine, and that which is cured by iron:
si est eclites soulement;	 this is only an exudate;
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	 and one should not use iron in these two resemblances:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	 that is to say, tympanites and ascites, because it is deadly;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	 therefore when you treat this resemblance of dropsy which is called «edema» with medicines, and the cure does not help, then see if the patient is weak, or if he has another illness besides dropsy, such as abdominal distension and similar things;
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	 If you do not touch it with iron, for there is doubt;
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	 and if you see the patient of great strength, and he has no other disease but only dropsy, and he is not too young nor too old, then thus should you work:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	 take the patient upright in your hands, and the attendant presses the belly at the lowest part of the foot, then take the thorny spatula according to this form:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	 And let it be cut from two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	 with its point, yet not so deeply that it could reach the intestines when inserted, and not injure it;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	 then observe if the dropsy is located towards the intestines:
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	 in this case, you must cut three fingerbreadths straight down below the elbow;
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	 And if the dropsy is due to liver disease, your incision should be on the left side of the navel, three fingers' width.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	 And if it is due to the spleen, then on the right side; and it is not necessary for the patient to lie upon the incision so that the excesses do not run to that weak place.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	 Then pierce all the skin with the instrument and push through, lifting your hand to all the subcutaneous tissue between the skin and the fascia, as if scraping, to the amount of one nail's width or around it.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	 Then pierce the fascia until the subcutaneous tissue comes into view, which is the place of water, then draw strongly, and insert this instrument in the shape of a hook.
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	 And it is similar to a fine silver chain, and is made of light brass or steel, and has at its lower part a small hole.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	 and on one side there are three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	 and two on the other side, and one on the other;
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	 and the head is cut like a quill, and it is the form of the incision that the scribe cuts into the quill:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	 at the top is the handle, so that when the instrument comes to the water, they now float on the instrument.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	 empty it therefore half or a third full, for if you empty more than necessary at that time, perhaps the patient may die from the loss of their spirit due to the weapon, falling into a coma or approaching death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	 mais according to the amount of its virtue, and according to what the disposition of the patient's virtue indicates, and his pulse.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	 then extract the instrument and hold the water, and it is now held by the heart which stops up the hole which is on the sponge, about which I have spoken, that you should pierce in this manner.
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	 then begin the instrument again the next day, if you see that the patient can endure this, and draw out a small quantity of water.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	 do this for some days, and beware not to let any more remain but just a little water.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	 And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave much water in him, then heal him with a burial or hot sand, and through much sweating or bathing in the sun, and let him drink wine.
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	 And the treatment with drying medicines until it is healed, and cauterize on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after extracting the fluid, as I have said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	 Of the obstruction of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	 Sometimes children are born without an opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	 If he needs to be pierced immediately with a very fine needle according to this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	 Then insert into the puncture a subtle plug of beeswax, and tie it and hold it thus for three days or four, and when it wants to make urine, let the plug be removed, and make urine, and then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	 And perhaps it is not necessary there, for the violent urine does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	 He whose opening is small, let him be treated with the linen cloth, as we have said, and it will widen.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	 Those who do not have the puncture in its proper place are harmed, for some are born with the puncture at the tip of the penis, which is why they cannot urinate forward unless they lift their penis upwards;
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	 And they cannot deceive because the material cannot reach the bone, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	 And the way to perform this is for the patient to lie on their back, then straighten the head of the rod and the handle so that they are even with the width of a feather quill, so that the hole meets in the middle as it should be;
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	 and beware of excessive bleeding that often occurs there, and if it happens, staunch it as one would staunch blood, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	 of the pustules on the rod
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	 Often these ablations come to the rod, and there is an appearance of ugly flesh;
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	 and some are malignant while others are not.
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	 So you must take them at one time with subtle pincers, cut and clean all of them, then apply damp cotton in an Egyptian ointment.
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then continue the cure of cleaning until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	 And if the bath is foul, of bad color and stinking, then it is necessary that you bring a cautery to it.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	 When you have cut it, and if the bandage is partly on the stick and partly outside, you must first remove the part of the bandage that is inside.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	 And when it is sewn together, then treat what is outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	 Because when you cure them together, it is not certain that the head of the stick will not be pierced, and blackness and corruption will occur in the stick and in the wound.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 So it is necessary to cut away all that is black and corrupted, then apply a plaster of honey and flour made from the bark of pomegranates and beans, then continue with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	 And if blood follows from bleeding, then apply the lunar cautery according to this manner.
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	 The cautery helps with two conditions together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	 that is to say, in the stopping of blood, and in the process of decay.
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	 And if the head of the bladder is rotten and retracted, then you must insert a lead pipe into the bladder's channel, and have the patient urinate through it.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	 And when the hair is thick at the head of the bladder, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, due to a wound or abscess, then you must carefully shave it with one instrument, until the tissue is freed and the head of the bladder is released on all sides.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	 And if it is difficult to remove this, then you must shave the top of the bladder and the skin with a spoon-like instrument.
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	 Then take a fine linen cloth soaked in cold water, place it between the two, and do not remove it again.
de la circoncision	 of the circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	 Circumcision is not a disruption of continuity like other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	 Nevertheless, when we perform this work by our will, especially on children, it is necessary that we do the best and lightest work for their salvation.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	 I say that the ancients did not speak of the circumcision of their children, for they do not practice it in their law, and we only know what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	 For I have seen that most of the masters and physicians who performed circumcisions did so on the penis, at the foreskin, and on the entire glans.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	 and blood flowed because there are two skins, and perhaps one was cut and the other remained.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	 Then it has to be recut, and the pain is double, and at the cleansing of the penis, the tip of the member is not assured;
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	 and in the cleaning of the nail perhaps the iron slips, and it ruins the work, and often it happens thus that there is no need for cleaning and I want it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	 From the mundification which is done with files, I have found the benefit of the experiment, because the files cut as well above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	 Because when you press your hand, cut equally in every part of the nail always;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	 but let the thread be well stretched around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	 and the manner of the first operation is such that you make the child, if it understands, think that you are only doing it to tie the thread around the nail, and then let him play in every way you can;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	 then hold it straight between your hands and hide the strength in your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see it, nor any of the instruments;
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	 Then put your hand on the rod and blow into the heart, and draw it upwards until the head of the rod is inside.
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	 Then clean it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then bind the place tightly with a double thread, then tie it under the fold to another loop.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	 And hold it with two fingers of the second knot at the wrist and index finger, and cut between the two ligatures, then lift the heart quickly and draw out the head of the rod.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	 Then let the blood flow drop by drop, for it is the remedy.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And apply powder over the wound, and on top of the powder place a cloth glued with a mixture of egg cooked in rose water, infused with good and fresh rose oil, and leave it there until the next day, and continue the treatment with another treatment until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	 The form of the strength for purification is this:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	 both heads should be sharp and cutting, and the heads should be as large as the hand equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	 The error in purification is when the heart escapes through the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	 Therefore, it is necessary that you extend it to your fingernail before the place makes an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	 and cut it equally, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then hold it with tweezers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	 And if they pass three days and that which is under the membrane is swollen, then leave it until such an abscess be appeased, and lightly scrape away the skin.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	 If you move the cutting edge as well as you can, be careful of the part of the rod, it will not harm him at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	 Then cure the place of a sudden wound with powder, as we have said in the treatment of powders, and if you cut into the heart too much and it goes upward, it will not harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 Then heal it, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	 regarding the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	 The retention of urine is due to the presence of stones, or frozen blood, or bone, or dead flesh, or similar things, as we have said in the division.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	 And if the urine is not released, and you see that the retention is due to a stone stuck in the neck of the bladder, then it is necessary for the patient to be bent over his knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	 And let the patient's feet be placed on his back, and extend his belly over the top of his back, and let the patient hold his breath as much as he can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	 And then the neck of the bladder is constricted for the expression of the stone above, causing the urine to be released.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	 And if it does not come out, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer an extraction with the entire instrument called a "syringe," which looks like this.
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	 And let it be of fine silver, lightly hammered, like a bird's feather;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	 And let the tube be one and a half palms long, and be thin at the top.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	 And the manner of urine flow is such that you take a double thread, and tie it to the top of a wool or cotton bag, and push the end of the thread into the syringe;
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	 and cut the excess wool and push it up to the end of the syringe, then grease the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and make the patient sit on a chair, and lift the bladder and penis with moist oil, olive oil, and warm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	 then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then fold the penis down towards the scrotum;
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	 then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and the patient will feel it approaching the empty space, and this is not done unless because the passage through which it goes is twisted.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	 Then they stretch the thread along all the wool tuft by tuft, and the urine follows the wool, then squeeze strongly, and make the urine run.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	 And start the syringe again until the bladder is emptied, and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	 Of the diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	 When there are scorching or blood in the bladder, or rotting is gathered there, and you put water and medicine to distill, do it all with an instrument called a “clepsydra”, which looks like this:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	 It is closed, and has three holes:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	 Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	 And the place where the instrument passes should be such that it tightly seals the penis without addition, so that one can draw out the moisture, and push when necessary.
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	 And when you see your medicine enter the bladder, put the tip of the cup in the moisture, and draw while it is inside.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	 If you extract the moisture from the socket, then firmly push the bone back in.
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	 The moisture will enter and go to the bladder immediately, causing the patient to feel it.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	 And this is the form of a subtle enema with which one gives an enema to the bladder:
si est ci:	 Here it is: ène
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	 It is made of silver or brass and has a higher head.
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	 And underneath the shoulder where the ligaments fall.
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	 Then take a sheep's bladder and put the moisture in it to enema the bladder, then tie it between the two breasts firmly with a double thread, and warm the pouch with that moisture on the fire.
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	 Then insert the head of the enema into the penis, then press your hand on the bladder so that all the moisture enters at once until the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	 And if you do not have a bladder, then take a piece of parchment, and make a circle out of it, and pierce it roundly all around.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	 Then put a strong thread through these holes, then assemble the circle like an almond, and put inside what you wish of oil and moisture and water, and tie it to the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	 And do as you did with the bladder, by pressing in your hand until the moisture comes into the bladder.
de la piere	 of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	 We have already said in the division the ways of stones and their extraction along with medications;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	 And I have said the difference between the infected stone like gravel, and all the signs, and in which stone one should work by cutting.
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	 And in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	 And I will tell you openly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	 I say that the stones which are found in the bladder are more common in children, and this is a sign that the water has leaked from the bladder, similar to water in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	 And it opens the urethra, and it makes the patient's penis swell, and he urinates frequently, and then it becomes inflamed;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	 And in many of these cases the foundation is lost.
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	 And healing is easy in children up to the age of four, and it is very serious in the elderly, and it is in moderate degree for those who are between youth and old age.
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	 And the treatment is lighter for those who have a large stone, than for those who have a small one.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	 And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with an enema, in order to draw out all the impurities that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	 Because sometimes it hinders in seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	 Then take the patient by the feet and lift him up and move him downward, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and it will jump out from the high place sometimes;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	 Then have him sit between your prepared hands, and his hands should be under his thighs, so that the bladder is entirely tilted downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	 Then search for it and touch it inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	 If you feel the stone in the area, then quickly proceed to cut into the stone now.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	 And if it does not fall out from being touched at all, then moisten your finger with oil from the left hand, if the patient is a child, or your middle finger, if the patient is a grown youth;
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	 And it thrusts it into its base, and seeks the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, then guide it to the neck of the bladder.
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	 Then press upon it with your finger, and thrust it out from there where you wish to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	 And instruct the assistant to press the bladder with his hand, and command him to extend with his right hand the testicles upwards, and with his left hand remove the skin that is beneath the testicles in the place where one makes the incision.
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	 Then insert the catheter there, of which this is the form:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	 And make an incision between that which is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the scrotum.
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	 And let it be straight on the stone, and your two thumbs should always be on the base, and the cutting edge should be made so that it is wide outside, and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	 perhaps the pressure of the thumb on the base will cause it to jump out suddenly without effort.
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	 and know that there are certain stones which have angles and edges:
si est griés a issir;	 if you cut into them, they can cause injury.
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	 And there are some which lie below, similar to a bean, round, from which the passage is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	 Therefore, for those with angles and edges, make the cut larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	 and if it does not jump out, then you must use tweezers that are like a file at the end, to pull out the stone so that it does not escape.
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	 where you place below it a subtle instrument, curved at the tip
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	 and if you cannot insert it thus, then enlarge the opening of the wound, and if the flesh tears, bind it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	 and if there are more than one stone, then place the largest first at the neck of the bladder, then cut into it, then draw it out forcefully, and the smaller ones afterwards if there are any more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	 And if it is very large, then it must be sewn shut, and make a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	 because two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	 either he dies, or the urine continuously flows through where the lesion cannot heal.
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	 but nevertheless, strive to extract it, or by breaking with pincers, until you remove it in pieces;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	 And when you have completed your work, fill the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and bind it, and place on top a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water, to cool the hot abscess.
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	 Then bind the patient on their neck, and do not unbind the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when you dislocate it, wash very well the place with oil and water, then treat it with ointment of lavender and ointment of basil until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	 And if such abscesses and corrosion occur in the wound, and if blood coagulates in the bladder, causing the urine to be retained in this manner that it does not pass with the urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	 then put your finger into the wound and draw out that blood, for if it remains, it will corrupt the bladder.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then lift the wound of water and oil and silk, and help him in all ways you know until he is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	 And it is necessary that at every hour you care for him, you tie the two thighs together and gather the medicines on the place.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	 And if the stone is small, and it is in the channel of the penis, and stuck in, and the urine cannot come out.
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	 so that the care I speak of now, that you cut it many times, is released from the cutting by this care.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	 I have already proven so.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	 Take an iron rod according to this shape, and it should be fitted with three pointed tips at one end:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	 then take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone, so that it cannot return into the bladder.
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	 then push the drill into the penis gently, until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	 And turn the auger towards your hand in the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from the other side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	 Soon the urine will come out, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the bladder.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	 Then it is immediately broken and jumps out with the urine, and the patient is cured;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	 And if you cannot do this because of any obstacle, then tie a thread under the stone and another on top, then make an incision in the bladder where the stone is between the two threads, then pull it out forcefully, and untie the thread, and clean the congealed blood that is in the wound; ‌
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And cure him until he is healed.
de la piere des femmes	 of the woman's stone
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	 Poc it happens that stones are in women, and if this occurs, the cure is difficult, and it is prohibited for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	 One reason is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	 And the second is that one cannot find a woman well-trained who exposes herself to physicians, especially when she is modest.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	 And the third manner is that perhaps one cannot find a woman well-versed in this manual art;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	 And the fourth manner is that the woman's stones are deeper than the man's stones, so it requires a deeper cut, and there is great fear. And if necessity demands this, then you must take a well-versed midwife, and rarely does one find her, and if you cannot find one, then seek a subtle and modest physician;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	 And it presents a wise midwife in the life of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and instructs her to do what you command her concerning the investigation of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	 and looks very carefully if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	 then she must put her finger in the vagina and seek the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	 and if she finds it, she constrains it under her finger, and recommends that she insert her finger in the vagina of the patient, and seeks and presses her left hand strongly on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	 If she finds it, she must move it little by little from the entrance of the bladder downwards until it reaches the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	 then cut on the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the knee, where it is moved and positioned, and you will feel the stone in that part.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	 and do not move your finger on top of the stone or beneath it, and let the first cut be small;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	 then insert the reed into the cut, if you feel the stone so narrow the wound that the stone may come out stronger, and know that there are many types of stones.
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	 namely, small and large, sharp and smooth, long and round, and those with roots.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	 If you know the signs, you will know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	 And if the blood overcomes you, apply powdered vitriol to the spot, and keep it there for an hour until the blood is stanched.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	 Then return to your work until the stone is weakened, and have the instruments that I told you about for the extraction of stones in men to assist you in your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	 And if the blood defeats you and it is from the artery that has been cut, then place the powder on the site and apply a tourniquet and bandages, and do not attempt this again, and leave the stone alone and do not extract it, for fear the patient might die;
puis cure la plaie.	 Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	 And when the heat of the blood is calmed and the place is dry, return to your work until the stone is broken.
de hernie carnouse	 of flesh hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	 Rancid humour is nothing other than a collection of moisture or white sap under the heart of the kidneys that contains the egg.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	 And it is called "sap", and sometimes it is properly in the web of the egg, so that one might think it is another egg.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	 And this is the skin of the knee among the white tissues which we have mentioned.
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	 And this does not happen unless there is pus.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	 And the generation of this ramice is due to weakness in the testicles, causing that substance to spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	 And sometimes it comes from striking the knee, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	 where it is a yellowish color or without red, or black, or watery white, and this happens most often;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	 And these are the signs to recognize this collection, for if it is in the white tissue which we have mentioned, then the abscess is reasonable, and the pus is long like the shape of an egg, and the knee does not open, because there is moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	 And if there is moisture in the very tissue, then the abscess is reasonable with one part of the egg, and because of this it seems that it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	 And if moisture is between the skin of the legs and the white flesh, it is felt well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	 Therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test all the introduced material, from which the form comes before.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	 According to what follows after the intromission, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	 And when we treat it with iron, it is necessary that the patient be bled according to our ability and the fullness of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	 then have him lie on his back, on something a little high, and place many blankets under him.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	 then sit on his left side, and command the attendant to sit on the right, and extend the rod to one of the two ribs at the hip.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	 then take the lancet, and cut the skin of the thighs lengthwise from top to bottom, almost to the bone, and let your incision be straight, dividing the skin of the thighs down to the white flesh, and delicately scrape according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	 Then pierce the sponge full of water with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then place your thumbs, and lift the sponge up.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	 and do not touch the center of the thumbs, but only the sponge;
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	 cut it all or in pieces like this, that if you do not cut well and skillfully, the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	 and if the water jumps too much for your work, then reset it in its place when you have completed the sponge's work.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then sew the two lips of the thumbs together with a stitch, then treat it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	 And if you find the water corrupted by another illness, then it is necessary to bind the vessels that are hanging down, suspecting the flow of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	 Then cut the testicles with all the suspensory apparatus, and remove the egg, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	 And if there is an artery assembled in two parts together, know that these are two arteries;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	 then cut the other part similarly to how you did the first equally, then wipe away the blood, and put moistened wool in rose oil on the wound;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	 and put another moistened wool in wine and oil, and place it on the two testicles, and put double cloths on top, and tie it up tightly all over with the bandage that follows this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	 Then take two cloths, and stuff them with shredded wool according to this appearance and sew them together in the crotch of the breeches, and one end should reach up to the buttocks, and the other to the groin area;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	 and let the other two heads rest on the two angles, and let all the reinforcement be gathered into the loop of the bridle;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	 and sometimes this thread is cauterized in place of an iron incision, which is to take a fine, subtle cautery knife, cut the skin of the scrotum, and heat it as we have said, so that the white layer containing the water is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	 take the cautery in this form, and pierce that layer at the testicles, and peel it with this heated subtle cautery;
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	 And cut in all ways you can, until you have shaved everything clean;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	 and be careful that the fire does not touch the testicle;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	 And know that this work is more effective;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	 And take care to avoid bleeding, and be aware of the operations of surgery;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	 And if anything goes against you, whether an abscess or bleeding or anything else, then treat what is going against you, according to what was said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	 And if the patient is fearful and does not wish to undergo this operation because of its horribleness, then use perforation, as I tell you, and it is that when you are certain by the signs we have spoken of that aquatic water is there, then make the patient sit on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	 Then pierce the abscess in the lower part as wide as possible, and insert the perforation into the length of the body;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	 And let the holes be wide so that all the water flows freely.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	 Then put cotton on the place, and tie it, and let the rest of the water drain, then treat until the wound is healed.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	 And if the white cloth does not let the water out at the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to draw water from dropsical patients, as described above.
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	 And widen the opening of the wound, and know that the water will return, and it will collect again after six months or around that time, and when it has collected like before, then the patient will pass his days thus.
de l’aposteme des coions	 of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	 Know that in cutting this vessel there is fear in many cases, so it seems better to leave it alone.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	 And I will tell you about the operation and similarities of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	 I say then that many abscesses come in the body, especially in the kidneys;
et c’est par mout de cas.	 and this is very common.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	 This is to say by excessive acidic and sharp humor that spreads to the kidneys, or from bruising;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	 and the color of the abscess depends on the body's color;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	 and it feels no pain, yet the abscess is serious;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	 and sometimes it is a painful and perilous abscess of red color, which can come from a clot in the artery, or an inflammation of the vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	 When it is from a clot in the artery, it is known by the hot state of the abscess when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	 And you must not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	 That which is made of a vein inflammation is known by its tendency to express upon the touch of fingers, and one can well make an incision on this appearance, and on other wounds;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	 And it is that you cut the heart of the testicles, then lift up the egg, and draw out the white thread, and free the supporting structure from all parts of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	 If the egg is already solidified with these wounds, then it is necessary that you draw out the egg and cut it;
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	 And if it is adhering to the thread or that which is inside the vessels, then you must free all of this thread and cut it roundly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	 And if the base of the flesh is in the rear place, then you must cut it all, and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And when your work is completed, fill the wound with wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then cure it with other remedies until he is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	 of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	 This is a type of abscess enveloped in an envelope similar to a bud, with the softening of the testicles, and if the patient moves severely while walking;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	 and the treatment of this disease is almost as frightening as that mentioned above, nevertheless we will tell you about its procedure according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	 You must make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then pass the scrotum between your legs, taking all the vessels near the penis, and hold them firmly, and stretch them greatly;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	 then cut with a broad spatula across the vessels until they are exposed, and then scrape from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the temporal arteries;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	 Then take a needle with a double thread, and tie it at the first place where the vein is located, and tie it again at the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	 Then cut them in half straight down, according to the length of the body, and draw out the corrupting moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	 Then treat the wound as with others where a bone is broken, so that some vessels are cut which nourish one of the bones.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	 because this way there is no harm, and if it happens to all the vessels, then the bones must be pulled for all the vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	 so that the bone does not lose its nourishment from the cutting of the vessels, and dries up and cannot help itself.
de la routure dou syfac	 of the rupture of the shoulder
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	 The happenings of this ramice are by the section that comes in the hypogastrium, or the extension on the belly in the area of the groin, because the intestines descend from that opening to one of the testicles.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	 And this opening is in the hypogastrium or in its extension, and these two types come from many causes:
