ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	 Or from a blow, or a jump, or a fall, or from lifting a heavy weight, and by similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	 And the signs when it is of the extension in the hypogastrium are that it happens gradually, over a long time, and does not come suddenly;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	 And the abscess is equal up to almost its full length, because the hypogastrium presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	 And the sign is when it comes from the section of the hip, which brings sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscess has a diverse appearance, beneath the skin near, and this is due to the exit of the intestines and the body lacking in the hip area.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	 And sometimes the coils come out with the intestines and are retained within, causing great pain for the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	 And in these cures by iron, there is fear, so one must avoid them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	 And the manner of working is that you instruct the patient to pull out the intestines with his hand into the wound, if he can reach in.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	 Then have him sit up on his neck. Between your hands, and lift the thighs;
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	 Then press the heart downwards, and cut all the skin of the testicles along their length;
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	 Then insert into the flanks of the loins stitches according to what you need to open the wound, and let it be such that the bone can come out;
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	 Then scrape off the tissue that is under the skin of the testicles, until the hard white tissue is exposed on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	 Then insert your finger between that which follows the testicle, between the white tissue under the skin of the egg, and the second tissue, and separate that which is behind the egg, and into the second tissue; xspace
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	 And then move to the right hand within the heart of the thighs, and stretch the white silk upward to your left hand, and lift the egg all along the silk towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	 And command the assistant to stretch the egg upwards, and untie that which is tied behind the bandage;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	 And ask your two assistants if there is any intestine wrapped in the white silk, and if you find anything, throw it into the stomach below.
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	 Then take a needle with a thread made of ten threads, and thrust it into the rear part of the silk, which is after the skin of the thighs.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	 After the waist, then cut the threads that appear from the silk, until there are four threads.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	 Then assemble them one on top of the other in the manner of a cross, and tie there the sinew that we have said is under the skin of the thighs, with a strong cord from two parts.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	 Then wrap the heads with threads and tie them strongly from two parts, so that none of the vessels that nourish them can enter within, lest an abscess form there.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	 And put back the cord according to the first long cord two fingers from that one, and after these two cords leave hanging the sinew that is under the skin of the thighs by a finger.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	 And then the other according to the roundness that the egg bears.
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	 Then cut in the part which is under the skin of the thighs until the blood runs and flows as we have said before.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	 Then introduce moistened wool in oil, and put it on wounds, and there introduce the ligature that we have mentioned.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	 And sometimes the white part is cauterized as we have said, after the incision, out of fear of blood loss.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	 For this happens often, and leave the ligature in place until it spontaneously falls off;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	 And if it delays falling off, then it should be washed with hot water, and put on what we have mentioned, until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	 Then treat the wound with another treatment, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	 of flesh hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	 In this ramus, I have never seen anyone who dared to make the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	 And the ancients said that it is done like the knot that is together with the string, in such a manner that you tie the vessels, after the cut lightly on the bottom side;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	 Then cut in half and treat the abscess with what is effective until the vessel falls out;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	 Sometimes there is a rupture in the veins, as we have said, and it opens the place;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	 and none of the intestines come out, and if they do, it is little, and it recovers every hour;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	 however, if it stays too long in this state, the wound or fistula swells until the intestines come out;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	 and this happens because of the expansion of the fistula in the veins, as we have said, for it is expanded, then the place becomes soft and swollen and open;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	 and the treatment is by cautery, as we have previously said;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	 And sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	 and the patient should lie on their back between your hands, then strike the swollen area of the dislocation with a width according to the size of three fingers.
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	 then remove the fascia that is under the skin and place the bandage on the visible part of the fascia.
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	 and press firmly on the stomach, then stitch the two visible parts of the fascia on top of the bandage, and sew one to the other.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	 then remove the bandage and do not strike the fascia or stretch it or anything else, as I have told you in the treatment of the hernia of the intestines.
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	 Then the treatment through the treatment of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 And when you cut the threads, so cleanse and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	 The silk is tight, and has no appearance in the suture, and the cautery is more effective in this place, and closer to health.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	 of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	 Often the skin of the testicles is soft in some men, because the vessels within are relaxed, and it is easy to see.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	 And it is necessary that when one wants to cure [it], one makes the patient lie on their back, and cut the softened skin onto the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	 Then join the two lips with a single stitch, and if you wish, first sew the excess skin in three or four tight stitches.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	 Then cut between the stitches, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	 For the incision
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	 Know that castration is condemned in our law, and therefore I would rather not speak of it in this book.
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	 And it is necessary to perform for two reasons:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	 the first being that the doctor knows how to respond when asked and knows the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	 and the second is that we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and deer and other animals.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	 Therefore, I say that castration is performed in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	 either by attraction or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	 In the method we perform by attraction, we make the animal sit in hot water until the testicles are softened and hanging;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	 then take them with your hand as far as they can go and until you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	 About the castration of size:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	 It is necessary that you dye the beast, and press its skin against your left hand, then tie the string, and strike on each hoof with one blow, when you have well skinned them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	 and leave any pouch of fat or the subtle fat that is over the vessel;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	 and this method of castration is better than that done by attraction, because in attraction some parts of the skin may remain, which causes the beast to desire lust;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	 then heal the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	 of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	 Hermaphroditism occurs in men in two ways:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	 one is that between the two testicles appears something similar to the natural figure of a woman, where there is hair, and sometimes urine flows from it.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	 And the other method is for women, and it is placed on the wrist like a rod and two cubits long.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	 And the treatment for both men and women is such that you cut the cartilages close together, and treat them like other wounds.
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	 In the second method, for men whose urine flows through the skin of the scrotum, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	 Of the fever
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	 A tonsure is a cartilage close together on the natural part, as long as it is too ugly to look at;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	 and some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	 You should dye the excess of the tonsure with your hand or scissors, and cut it lightly;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	 and do not go too deep, lest blood comes out, then treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	 And for another type that is born at the mouth of the womb, and it swells, and perhaps it jumps strongly, and it resembles a cow, and therefore the ancients called it "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	 If it is necessary, you must cut it off, as we have said about the tendon, and treat it until it heals.
de erratique	 of error
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	 It is erratic when the woman's nature is not understood, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	 and it is either a natural birth defect, or an accident caused by illness that has occurred.
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	 Or it is due to a nearby object, or from subtle or thick smoke, and it is formed in the womb, either on one side, or below, or wherever. )))
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	 And it prevents conception, and childbirth, and perhaps even menstruation.
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	 And the knowledge of this comes from the examination by the healer.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	 If the swelling is imminent, it will appear at your thumb or foot.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	 If it is of subtle syrup, and it is near two pounds, then hasten, and let them be like this:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	 Place your two thumbs together, and let the woman be on her back, with her legs spread.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	 Then weigh out the two pounds firmly, so that the subtle syrup is round, and cover it well.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	 Then take wool, soak it in oil, and place it on the spot, and let the woman lie down every day, so that it may not heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	 And if the syfac is hard and thick, you should cut it with a spatula similar to a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	 If the covering is of fresh meat, then suspend it at the knee and cut into it.
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	 And have the medicines that staunch blood, such as agrimony, dragon's blood, frankincense, together with plenty of egg. xspace
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	 then bring a broad lead plate, so that the wound cannot close.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	 and let it be so for a long time, and bring him a tent of dry linen;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then he should be treated with other treatments until he is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	 And when in the flesh comes a boil, it must be covered in this manner, if it is not an infected abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	 For an infected abscess that is in the flesh, one should not touch or make with fire.
des emorroides	 of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	 Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that usually appear without a cause, and when hemorrhoids are old they become hard;
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	 and we have already said in the section the similarities of them, and the signs, and I will say here those which receive treatment.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	 I say that hemorrhoids and hardened ones, when they are deeply embedded in the flesh and do not appear to the touch, are not cured by fire.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	 Those who are at the edge of death, which can be felt, are those whom one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	 Therefore, you must place the woman in a cold house. Then press down on it with pliers and cut off its roots, then powder medicines that restrain blood flow, such as acacia and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	 Then he puts his feet against the wall for an hour, then places them in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	 And if blood comes out, then she makes her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate bark and galls and similar things, and then takes barley flour, and mixes it with honey and oil, and makes an emplaster on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	 And if it bleeds, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	 If not, she has him aerate cupping glasses on his back and breasts without piercing the skin.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	 Then she takes linen, moistens it with plantain juice or hawthorn juice with old wine, and aerates in place.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And when the abscess subsides, she treats the place with oil until it is healed;
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	 And that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles a sharp head, so you must cover it as I have said for the telul.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then heal until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	 of the abscesses of the uterus
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	 Many types of abscess occur in the uterus, such as canker, purulent abscess, herpes, cysts, fistulas, hemorrhoids, and hot abscess, and many other diseases that I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	 It must therefore be said in this treatise about the hot abscess that comes to the breast, which is not one of the abscesses that swell well.
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	 And if you wish to know the ironwork, look whether the abscess is sharp at its beginning, and full of heat and fever, and if it turns red, if you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	 Then do not hasten to pierce, but let the abscess ripen until the pain is relieved;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	 And then make the patient sit on a chair, and have two small chairs where he leans back, and support his back and bring together his feet at the outer parts of the thigh;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	 And let his thighs be spread wide, and place his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good cord;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	 Then give him to drink towards the right side, and bring there the instrument with which one works the opening of the wound, from which afterward comes the form;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	 And it is necessary that when you see this instrument being brought there, that you first insert the ray to know the depth of the wound, so that what enters from the instrument does not go deeper than it should, and does not injure the patient;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	 And if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloths so that the instrument does not hurt it;
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	 And it is necessary for him to place the horn of the instrument above, and to dip the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	 And when the abscess opens, and one makes an opening with the soft hand, it must be covered at the top with spongy cloth.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	 And when the abscess is emptied, it is necessary that you place in the wound tents moistened in rose oil, or in dry green oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	 And place the tent further into the wound at the bottom of the sore, and place over the sore and over the finger a clean cloth moistened in water or cooked mallows.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	 Then the care after two days of oil application to this extent, until it is healed.
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	 and sometimes one lifts the scab and the wound with a clyster of water and honey, and then with water and long roots of iris and elecampane cooked;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	 then return to oil application.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	 Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.
de l’enfantement	 of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	 It is necessary first for the midwife to know the figure of natural childbirth, and the signs are when you see the woman press down below, and desire to smell air.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	 then quickly the child is about to issue forth;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	 therefore know that this birth is according to natural form, and the outlet is under its head, and the afterbirth with it.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	 And when you see these signs, it is necessary to gently press his belly, so that the child comes out quickly.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	 because when he descends upon his head, the afterbirth follows with him, and the mother is cleansed of her excesses by good cleansing.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	 and this one who comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	 Because sometimes he comes feet first, and sometimes the body or head comes out strongly, or the hands, or he comes out on his back, or sometimes upside down, and by chance he is turned onto his neck, and in other evil forms.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	 so it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skillful in these things, and to guard against error and deception, and I will show you all the forms how she must help him.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	 If a child comes out headfirst by natural birth, and the woman gives birth painfully, and her strength is weak, then make her sit on a stool, where women hold her.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	 and let some oil or fenugreek be cooked, then the midwife puts between her teeth the small spoon which has this shape:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	 and tear open the afterbirth, and cut to her nail so that the moisture inside flows out;
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	 and press the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must enema the woman with fenugreek muslin mixed with sesame oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	 then make her inhale and sneeze condiments, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	 If one extracts the child now.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	 And if the two hands come out strongly, then you must reset them gently piece by piece;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	 and if they cannot enter, then place the woman on a seat, and lift her feet up high;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	 then take away the seat from under her, and hold the woman so that she does not fall during this process.
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	 And if the hand cannot enter and the child is dead, then cut off the hands with a knife that was placed before, extract the child, and reset accordingly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	 of the child's exit onto its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	 When the child comes out on its feet, one must push it upwards;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	 and then turn him little by little until he is even.
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	 Then take hold of his feet and stretch them little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	 When he can jump up to his knees, have him grasp it and sneeze with condiments.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	 if he jumps further, so be it by God's will.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	 And if he does not jump as high as we have said, then turn him little by little until he is according to the natural figure.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	 Because then he will be light.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	 And if he does not come further as we have said, then take mace from an almond tree, and sesame oil, and melted gum, and grind everything together in a mortar.
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	 apply this ointment over the woman's genital area and on the outside as well. Then make her sit in hot water up to her ribs.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	 and when she is sufficiently moistened below, give her a mustard plaster and place it below, leaving it on for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	 Then make her sit on the seat, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and press lightly on her belly, for the child jumps now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	 Of the delivery of the child upon its knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	 When the child comes in this form, then the midwife places her hands little by little;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	 and she is made to sit on his neck, and her feet hang down, and she lies on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	 and folds her hands little by little, and then takes hold of the hands on top of the belly, and removes the cushions from below, so that she is ready to descend.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	 And if the child does not jump, then take his feet and move them strongly, then move the belly upwards, then put your hands in.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	 And feed the child little by little;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	 And instruct the woman to take [care] until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	 Of the delivery of the child that comes with one hand hanging down
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	 It is necessary to devise a method to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	 if it cannot be brought back, then have the woman get up and walk;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	 If she cannot walk, then have her lie down on a bed, and spread her legs widely;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	 Then bring the midwife that I mentioned;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	 and if she does not deliver, have her sit on a stool, then consider how to bring back the hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	 and feed the child according to natural figure, and make him sneeze, and instruct her to take [care] until the child comes out strongly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	 of the emergence of the child from its neck, and its hands extended, and its face turned towards the back of its mother
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	 It is necessary that the nurse wash their hands, then turn the cup little by little, and pour gently.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	 And when it is equal, place on the natural mixture of althea and oil, as we have said, then instruct her to move little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	 And when you have done this, make her sit on the seat and command that she rest.
et la fai esternuer.	 And make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	 In this same manner, for all the second stage
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	 When the mucus comes out in this manner to all the nostrils, then cut the nostril with your nail until the moisture is emptied.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	 And if the child cannot breathe through its face and neck, then cut from below, so that it is not retained, and let the child die.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	 then put the child inside, as much as you need to place it, and instruct the woman to take some time:
adonques si istra legierement.	 then draw it out gently.
de l’issue des gemelz	 of the birth of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	 Know that twins are often born, and sometimes three or four are born.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	 And this is not a strange thing, and it happens rarely.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	 Two is a strange thing, and they do not live, except rarely; 》
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	 I know that being multiple is a defect, and they are deprived of the fluid that divides them, which is connected to the belly; 》 》
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	 And sometimes they come out as naturally as any other, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	 And if they come out violently, then treat it as we have said, and let the midwife be skilled, and do quickly and lightly what she does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	 And make sure to do this as if you are going for safety.
de plusors enfans	 of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	 Sometimes they are formed in the womb I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII, or more up to XV, and all are shaped like a child by the measurement of the wise glorious one, and it is necessary that the midwife knows all these things, for by chance similar things may happen to her;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	 And do so according to what is needed.
de l’enfant mort	 of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	 When you cure the woman of a dead child or miscarriage, as I have said in the division, and it does not come out on its own, and you are forced to work with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	 Then you must know if the woman is of sound virtue, and does not have an illness or fear of death.
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	 So it must happen that the woman is placed on her back, and her head inclined downward, and her legs raised.
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	 And let the midwife apply the tincture in two places, where she is bound to the bed so that she cannot move during childbirth.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	 Then rub the mouth of the pregnant woman with moistened oil, blended with althea and fenugreek and flaxseed, then let the midwife anoint her hands with these oils and herbs.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	 Then gently insert them into the pregnant woman, then seek the place where she inserts the unguents so that they may be suitable for this purpose, and take care that the child is prepared to descend onto its head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	 If he thrusts the dagger in his eyes or his neck or his mouth or under his palate or beneath the beard or in the throat or near the ribs, and if the descent is on the feet, then he should thrust in the sole or in the sides.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	 and it is necessary that he holds the dagger in his right hand, and places the handle between his left thumb and forefinger, and strikes with all his might, and thrusts the dagger into any of these places that we have mentioned, until it reaches the empty space;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	 and this is the shape of the dagger.
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	 Then thrust against another dagger, or a third if you need it, so that the extraction is equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	 And then they are made equal by moving to and fro, so that the bone may issue forth, and let the claws be toothed to hold it, as in this form.
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	 And if some part remains, then let the surgeon anoint two of his fingers with oil and push them into that part, and draw out the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	 And if nothing remains, then place this claw in a higher location, and do the same until all comes out.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	 And if one hand comes before the other and cannot be brought back due to swelling, then you must wrap it in a cloth until it all comes out.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	 Then cut it into the joint of the sole or at the heel, and so you must do with the other hand and both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	 And if the head of the child is large and it is narrow at the exit, or if there is sharp water collected at the head, then you must insert a pointed catheter between your fingers, puncture the head, and extract the water.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	 or you can use an instrument called "almidach", with which the forms come with the instruments or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	 and do the same if the child naturally has a large head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	 and then draw the bones with forceps, and if the head jumps out strongly and sticks in the birth canal, it should be split until the moisture that is in the worst exit comes out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	 and if it cannot come out, cut it into pieces as you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	 And if he is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce him so that the moisture runs out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	 And if the child is on its feet, then the traction is light, and the application to the mother's mouth is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	 And if he is constricted in the belly or in the breast, then you must stretch him on a cloth wrapped around your hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	 and cut open the belly or the breast, so that the moisture within runs out.
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	 and if the other members are removed, and only the head remains, then the surgeon should insert his hand into the wound deeply, and pull it out until it reaches the mouth of the wound.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	 Then he places one or two sponges therein, and pulls them out strongly.
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	 And if the mouth of the wound is constricted due to a hot abscess that has formed there, then one must not work on it, but rather apply moist and greasy substances.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	 And let the physician prepare poultices, and boil them in softening and moistening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	 And if the child is on his side, and you can place him flat, then prepare as we have said for a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	 And if one cannot, then draw out the cord piece by piece, and leave nothing of the membrane.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	 And when you have done this, let the physician prepare what we have said for abscesses that come in marriage;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	 And if blood discharge occurs, then place it in restraining water, and let the physician prepare other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	 And I saw a woman in whose womb one child had died, and then another was conceived on top of it, and that other also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	 After a long time, he developed an abscess on the thigh, which swelled until it burst, and began to exude greatly.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	 I was called to treat it, and thought about it for a long time, but the wound could not be healed.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	 I applied a strong drawing plaster, and from it came out a bone, and after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	 I was greatly amazed, for the belly has no bones at all.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	 So I thought that these were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	 I sought the wound, and removed many bones, until the woman was in a better state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	 And the woman lived for a long time thus, and always exuded a little pus from the place.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	 And I have not written this chapter except that, when the master finds something strange, he should know how to help it.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	 to bring the wound back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	 Here follows the form of the pressing instrument, with which we treat the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	 and at two turns, as the two heads of the two screws.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	 However, let the horn be more delicate than the press, and let it be made of boxwood or ivory;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	 and let the mouth of the stock be two fingers wide, and the edge of the boards one finger thick, and in length a palm and a half.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	 and between the two screws there should be two supports of this same wood, which are firmly attached to one another, half a palm long or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	 And these two adjustments are placed in the mouth of the horseshoe to open when one turns the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	 Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, should be made of ebony or boxwood, similar to the shape of tongs;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	 and it must have two adjustments at each end, as you see, one palm long and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	 and when you want to open the horseshoe with the entire instrument, make the woman sit on the bed with her feet hanging and legs spread, then place the two adjustments together in the horseshoe, and hold the head of the instrument underneath between her thighs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	 then work your hand with the entire instrument, just as you did with the tongs, according to the amount that you want to open the mouth of the horseshoe, until the hole is made as wide as you wish.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	 These instruments are all surpassed, and their likenesses are multiplied.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	 And when the doctor has prepared them, the work is all the more urgent, and higher in reputation among people because of their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	 Do not discard the instrument until you have prepared it, for their needs are not negligible.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	 When the secondine is used for childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath, then make her sneeze strongly, and hold your hands over her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	 And if she faints from this, that's a good sign.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	 If not, take a pot and make a hole in the lid, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cascara, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	 all these herbs, or some of them, be cooked in water on the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	 then put a reed or tube from the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the patient, and hold it until the steam enters the patient's mouth;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	 then make them sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	 If the ligament is cut quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	 And if it persists after this treatment and does not diminish, command the woman to wet her left hand in oil of cumin or a poultice of hollyhock, and then place it on the vulva, and seek for the discharge;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	 and when she finds it, take hold of it and pull straight and little by little, so that the patient does not shrink from the extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	 But one must move it gently to the right and to the left, then pull.
si venra et se desaerdra.	 It will come out and dislocate again.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	 And if the throat is narrow, we have said that the treatment is to sneeze, and with smoke from herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	 and if it does not come out with all that we have said, be careful not to pull too hard.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	 but it is necessary that what is at the throat, you tie to the thigh of the woman, then give her an enema with ointment quadruple.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	 It will rot and be reset, and it will come out stronger.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	 but still, when it rots, it causes a bad smell in the stomach and head, and harms the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	 It is necessary therefore for suitable fumigation for this.
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	 none of the ancients have proven fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	 The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to retain the flow and the afterbirth is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	 And it is like vinegar, and place the subtle part at the top, and the wide parts over the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	 and let the fumigation be above the coals, and continue until it is consumed, and then begin another one.
de percier lou fondement	 to pierce the anus
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	 Many children are born who do not have their anus pierced, but instead have a thin membrane covering it:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	 so it is necessary for the midwife to pierce this membrane with her finger, and do not pierce it with a sharp instrument, and be careful that she does not touch the wound.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then put on a damp cloth soaked in wine and oil, then treat with poultice until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	 And if you doubt that it will not stop, then put a piece of lead in the hole and leave it for less days, and let it be removed when the child wants to go into rooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	 And sometimes this happens suddenly from a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	 then it is necessary to cover that quickly:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	 if it is treated, as we have said about the poplar bud.
de la fistule dou fondement	 about the fistula of the anus
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	 Fistulas that come from under the anus are knots, and growths that come near the anus outside, or in the space of the two parts, if there is one fistula or several;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	 and when that knot is old, it works, and it brings with it moisture, white or subtle pus, and sometimes these fistulas are persistent;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	 And they are known by this: that there is an emission or flatulence when the patient has an emission, and sometimes one comes out as a fart.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	 And there are fistulas that penetrate to the bladder, and halfway down the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	 and reach as far as the junction of the thigh, and even to the head of the testicle.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	 And thus one recognizes a fistula penetrating the anus and not penetrating it:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	 and this is that you insert your index finger into the anus, and insert a fine needle of bronze or iron into the fistula when it is not twisted.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	 And if there is twisting, then insert a fine lead tent or a horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair with your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	 And if you do not feel it, and there is no passage of feces or gas or bile, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	 know that it has not perforated;
si te haste dou curer.	 then hasten to cure [it].
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	 Et when the fistula extends to the bladder or to the passage of the urine, then the urine leaks out, and it cannot be healed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	 If it is perforated as far as the junction of the thigh, the tent will come to that place;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	 if there is no twist and the discovery of pain around it, then it exits soon after, and neither medicines nor stitching through poultice are effective;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	 And in these Persian fistulas there is no cure except for labor, and the vanity of foolish doctors who meddle with them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	 In those that are not Persian and are not ancient, there is hope of health through iron, as I have proven, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on their back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	 And he lifts his legs up to his hips, and let his hips be inclined towards his belly.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	 Then place an iron tent or of lead if there is convulsion, so that you know where the tent comes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	 If the patient feels it around the anus, then you must put your index finger there, if you then feel that the tent has passed through.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	 And let it be uncovered where you sense between your finger the spleen or the flesh, then know that it is perforated.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	 If it cannot be treated, then do not bother with it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	 Nevertheless, it is said that some can be well healed, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	 And aid is done by heating the subtle cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	 and presses it all hot into the fistula, until it reaches near the anus;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	 and do this two or three times, so that you know these fleshy tissues are burned, which are like a bird's feather.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	 and then cure it with moist tents in butter, so that this flesh comes out, then cure with a salve of healing herbs and binding.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	 If he is thus healed, that is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	 If this, otherwise cannot be cured;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	 and if the tent enters, and does not reach to the finger in the anus, and between your finger and the tent there is a thick covering of flesh or sinew, and you see the fistula like this which follows the covering of the heart.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	 If from the beginning of the fistula, and always push forward the tent, and then after the cautery, until it comes to the head of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	 And the tent will be released and fall;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	 Then shave off those hairs that appear like a bird's feather, leaving nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	 And if the pus overcomes you and enters between you and the work, then cauterize it with fire or strong medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	 For the fire cautery brings together two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	 That is to say, the burning of these hairs, and the staunching of blood and drying out of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	 Then treat moist tents with butter or ground substance, until the place swells up, and the burned hairs come out of the swelling.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	 then cure the wound with sudorific onions and hard flesh, and the medicines are dry.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	 When it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	 And if the fistula reaches to the bottom of the anus and is distant from the body, then press your finger into the anus and inquire about it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	 If you feel the tent and inside there are either the fabric or the tarpaulin or the wood which is about to rot, then let there be only air that comes from faith and hope, through the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	 or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut to the bottom, or if you can do so place tents there and treat as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	 and do not go too deep, lest you cut the support that holds the foundation, and the discharge comes out there unwillingly.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	 then treat it as we have said.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	 par aventure si sera sanez, or you remove that covering and clean it once it is cut near the base, either by probing or with another suitable instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	 then cleanse that foul matter which is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	 then strive to restore the wound and to stop the fistula in the part below the base;
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	 if it would be easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	 And sometimes fistulas are of this kind:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	 and it is when you probe the fistula, and it is on the side of the base near the skin above, then take a probe pierced at the tip like this: ️
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	 And insert a twisted thread into it, and insert the tent with all the thread into the fistula until it reaches the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	 If it is passing through the edge of the base within, then draw out the thread from that hole, as you push your finger into the base;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	 And pull the thread end, and bring the two heads together, and hold one to the other, and leave it for one day or two.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	 And restrain it several times, so that the thread cuts through the flesh between them, and they fall off;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	 then treat the wound until it is healed and healthy.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	 Si la fistule ne perce pas, fais-la percer de toutes les manières possibles, sauf si elle est trop profonde.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 For it is not fitting to cover the wound too deeply with a cap, and then heal it, as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	 The shape of the sharp spine used to make a fistula is very sharp and cutting on one side;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	 and not on the other side, so that it does not cut what should not be cut, as you can see here.
des emorroydes	 from hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	 Embryos are according to two kinds:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	 or they are within the anus, like a grain of resin, and there are small ones and large ones, and it often bleeds, and there is one or more, and they are outside the anus and at the top of the anus.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	 Mais celles qui sont defuer ainsi ont peu de moiteur, et encore toujours ou un peu d'eau citrine ou un peu de sang, et elles ont la couleur du corps.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	 et le cure de celles qui les ont dedans le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malade qu'il s'essuie pour aller dans les chambres, jusqu'à ce que le fondement lui issu fuer, et que les fils apparaissent;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	 si tu t’empresses, et le prends avec des pinces, ou tu le tiens avec ton ongle, puis le coupes à sa racine.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	 et si les pinces ne peuvent pas les tenir à cause de leur moiteur, alors les prends avec un morceau de tissu, ou du coton, ou une pièce de chiffon.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	 And draw them to your teeth, then cut them off, and sprinkle some hot powders on top for the cautery;
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	 And cauterize them as it is said in the chapter on cautery, then treat with other treatments until they are healed;
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	 And if the base cannot come out, then use an enema for the patient with a biting and harsh enema to clean what is in the base, so that it can come out clearly;
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	 When the patient presses, and if the threads are out of the base, then the treatment is light;
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	 And it is that you take them with your nail or with pliers, and cut them off, then treat as we have said until they are healed, and let the patient fear the cutting with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	 It is necessary for you to suture according to this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	 Take a twisted thread, and put it in a needle, then pull the thread through the other side and make the needle pierce from another place, and turn the two ends of the thread underneath the needle, and let it be wide;
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	 And pull the thread tightly, then tie a knot in the thread, and remove the needle, and do so with all the others, and leave one to drain the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	 then place on top a damp cloth soaked in rose oil or in cerate, and place it on top, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And then let them alone until they fester, and when they have fallen off, treat the wounds with ointment and other treatments, until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	 Of dryness of the intestines or rectum
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	 Many times there is dryness in the intestines, due to natural constraint, and when the illness is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	 Si it is necessary that you remove with the tip of a scalpel or with your nail the scab on top, which does not let it moisten;
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	 then treat it until it heals as needed;
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	 and if it cannot heal, then begin the scraping again more strongly than before, until it heals well and is scabbed over.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	 then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	 Of trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	 A formica is a small hairy appearance under the skin, and it goes very deep;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	 and sometimes it finds the cold, and one feels it also as if dead from trembling, and it comes to the whole body, and more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	 And the treatment is that you take a quill of a goose feather, or a strong feather of a vulture, and place that quill on the trembling, so that the circle encloses the trembling all around.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	 Then turn your hand to the entire chain until you capture all around the trembling, and place it entirely, and pull out the trembling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	 And if you see, do this with a reed of brass or iron according to this form, and let it be subtle below and drawn above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	 Do not cut, in order to hold onto two, and press harder.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	 And if you see it, then cauterize the trembling, just as it is written in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	 of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	 Sometimes a silver enema or arsenic or melted bronze or iron can be made;
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	 and sometimes these instruments are made in small and large sizes according to those for whom they are prepared.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	 Therefore, those who are prepared for the treatment of children and who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	 The form of the small and large enema is wide at the top, where the intestines are tied in this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	 And if there is an obstruction where the intestines are tied as you see, and the end is pierced;
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	 And on one side, let there be two holes, and on the other side, one.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	 And let the belly where the medicines are placed be made from a beast's bladder or parchment, and let it be pierced all around with small holes, and there should be one finger's width between each hole. Then insert into these holes a strong thread of twisted linen, crossing in an X shape or around the belly, and gather the belly together like a goatskin;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	 And when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread at the front, then administer an enema.
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	 And this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	 And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold. Anoint the tip of the enema with oil or egg yolk, or a similar substance, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	 Then the servant squeezes it with both his hands until it is all clear, then he releases the enema, and the patient lifts his legs to the wall, and if the medication wants to come out, he holds it as much as he can;
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	 And if he sleeps through the night, it is even greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	 And if you enema him for a disease of the swollen belly, and the medicine hastens to come out, then repeat it until he is healed.
